    }

    }

        display: none;
    }

        border-top: 7px solid #0074a6;
    }

        border-right: 1px solid #e5ebee;
        content: attr(data-th);
        display: block;
        font-family: "Expert Sans Bold", Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;
        font-weight: normal;
        padding: 16px;
        position: absolute;
        bottom: 0;
        left: 0;
        right: 65%;
        top: 0;
    }

    TABLE:not([class]) tbody tr th:before {
        border-right: 1px solid #e5ebee;
        content: attr(data-content);
        display: block;

        font-weight: normal;

        top: 0;
    }
